msg:Ctrip‚Äôs self-operated parent-child room, the price of 708, is more reasonable than other parent-child rooms that cost thousands of dollars, but you get what you pay for. The children are quite satisfied with their requirements, and they also said that they will live in another room type with slides next time. However, the experience of adults is relatively poor, and the service and facilities are not up to standard. Let me declare that the picture is the state of check-out after we stayed, and the room we stayed in was cleaned.
1. The front desk is unprofessional, does not understand the facilities in the room, and asks for good reviews. For example, I asked if there was any disposable laundry detergent in the room, and I said no. We bought a bucket of laundry detergent outside, but found that there was one when we entered the room. Another example, the room card was left in the room, and I asked the front desk to help me copy a card, but the front desk asked me if the order was made by me, if I could give a good review, and asked to mention her name.
2. The facilities are too old, there are stains that cannot be removed on the bathroom glass and the bathtub table. You have to disinfect the bathtub yourself before using it. It is recommended to renovate if it can meet the hotel budget. Replace it with smart toilets and electric curtains. After all, Nanxiang is known as the best hotel. There is a bathtub in the room, and it is recommended to provide a disposable bathtub bag. It doesn't add much cost, but the tenant's check-in experience is really up.
3. Unprofessional cleaning, knocking on the door to urge you to check out. We had already called the front desk and agreed to check out at 2 o'clock, but the cleaning staff still knocked on the door to urge us to check out. This is really shocking.
4. The mini bar is empty, the refrigerator cannot be frozen, and the ice cream bought for children has melted. It is recommended to change the refrigerator and put a few bottles of drinks in the minibar.
5. It is recommended to change to a 2-meter bed, 1.8 is a bit crowded with children.
6. The elements of Big Mouth Monkey do not match the promotional content. There are monkey elements in the promotional photos of bath towels and towels, but they are not. The children's gift pack includes bathrobes, toothbrushes and children's slippers, but there is no children's shower gel, shampoo and children's toothpaste. Expectations and actual experiences are not equal.
7. The most satisfying indoor swimming pool, children like it very much, and guests can go there at any time. The hotel lobby is also a clearance. But referring to my comments above, the facilities and services really need to be improved to be worthy of such a lobby.
Just to make a statement, the minibar, disposable bathtub bags, children's supplies, etc., all of these have to be discussed with the front desk. question.

Generally speaking, families with low requirements for parent-child rooms can try to stay, after all, the price is there. However, if you travel without children, it is recommended to choose the nearby Baoshan Jiusi Hotel. I stayed for four nights in a row. The front desk there is very professional. The equipment is also very new, smart toilet electric curtains and Xiao Ai smart home, the management is humanized, the price is lower than here, and the check-in experience is comfortable.
The evaluation is harsh. After all, I have a comparison with Jiusi Hotel in my heart, and it is actually consumed, for reference.

msg:First of all, I would like to say sorry to the hotel. I didn't take many photos, but I wanted to write something, so the photos are just a few, and I hope the text is realistic.

I stayed here once on May 1st eight years ago. Of course, it was not called the current name at that time, and the service was not comparable, so let‚Äôs start with the hardware.

Although the owner has changed hands in the past eight years, the hardware facilities seem to have not changed. From the parking lot to the lobby, the decoration seems to be outdated, even though it is not particularly bright on a sunny day.

Walking into the room, the layout is still very reasonable, but the equipment and facilities in the bathroom are too old, even in 2023, you can only shower in the bathtub, and the basic dry and wet separation is not done. The quality still needs to be improved. Even if the price has increased during the holidays, the configuration of related toiletries should be at least a little higher than that of the Express Hotel.

The hardness of the mattress is moderate, even soft, but the quality of the pillows needs to be improved. Not to mention a variety of options, but at least two basic configurations, soft, hard, thick, and thin, should be available, otherwise you will fall asleep all night. It's too uncomfortable.

Fortunately, the gap in hardware has been greatly made up for in terms of service. From the answering of all questions at the check-in at the front desk, to the responsiveness of room service, and even to the telephone return visit after leaving the hotel, the attitude is first of all worthy of recognition, and secondly, the quality of service The decoration is also quite in place, giving people the feeling of home.

Finally, give me some advice:
1. It is possible to develop a richer level of food and beverages. Buffet options with higher cost performance are introduced for lunch and dinner, and even the breakfast itself can be richer in variety
2. Now that the parent-child hotel is positioned, you can take out the area that is really provided for children to play. The roof garden has not been opened during the whole stay

By the way, the swimming pool in the hotel is very good. You can watch the plane while swimming, and you can swim twice in 24 hours after check-in. It‚Äôs still very good. Generally speaking, for the service of the staff, I must still give it a full five-star rating. I hope that the guests‚Äô suggestions will also be good. Can be considered comprehensively.
